[Exodus 12:42](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/12?lang=eng&id=p42#p42) It is a night to be much observed unto the LORD for bringing them out from the land of Egypt: this is that night of the LORD to be observed of all the children of Israel in their generations. ^c12v42

[Exodus 12:43](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/12?lang=eng&id=p43#p43) ¶ And the LORD said unto Moses and Aaron, This is the ordinance of the passover: There shall no stranger eat thereof: ^c12v43

[Exodus 12:44](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/12?lang=eng&id=p44#p44) But every man's servant that is bought for money, when thou hast circumcised him, then shall he eat thereof. ^c12v44

[Exodus 12:45](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/12?lang=eng&id=p45#p45) A foreigner and an hired servant shall not eat thereof. ^c12v45

[Exodus 12:46](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/12?lang=eng&id=p46#p46) In one house shall it be eaten; thou shalt not carry forth ought of the flesh abroad out of the house; neither shall ye break a bone thereof. ^c12v46

[Exodus 12:47](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/12?lang=eng&id=p47#p47) All the congregation of Israel shall keep it. ^c12v47

[Exodus 12:48](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/12?lang=eng&id=p48#p48) And when a stranger shall sojourn with thee, and will keep the passover to the LORD, let all his males be circumcised, and then let him come near and keep it; and he shall be as one that is born in the land: for no uncircumcised person shall eat thereof. ^c12v48

[Exodus 12:49](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/12?lang=eng&id=p49#p49) One law shall be to him that is homeborn, and unto the stranger that sojourneth among you. ^c12v49

[Exodus 12:50](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/12?lang=eng&id=p50#p50) Thus did all the children of Israel; as the LORD commanded Moses and Aaron, so did they. ^c12v50

[Exodus 12:51](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/12?lang=eng&id=p51#p51) And it came to pass the selfsame day, that the LORD did bring the children of Israel out of the land of Egypt by their armies. ^c12v51

[Exodus 13:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/13?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) AND the LORD spake unto Moses, saying, ^c13v1

[Exodus 13:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/13?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) Sanctify unto me all the firstborn, whatsoever openeth the womb among the children of Israel, both of man and of beast: it is mine. ^c13v2

[Exodus 13:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/13?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) ¶ And Moses said unto the people, Remember this day, in which ye came out from Egypt, out of the house of bondage; for by strength of hand the LORD brought you out from this place: there shall no leavened bread be eaten. ^c13v3

[Exodus 13:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/13?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) This day came ye out in the month Abib. ^c13v4

[Exodus 13:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/13?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) ¶ And it shall be when the LORD shall bring thee into the land of the Canaanites, and the Hittites, and the Amorites, and the Hivites, and the Jebusites, which he sware unto thy fathers to give thee, a land flowing with milk and honey, that thou shalt keep this service in this month. ^c13v5

[Exodus 13:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/13?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) Seven days thou shalt eat unleavened bread, and in the seventh day shall be a feast to the LORD. ^c13v6

[Exodus 13:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/13?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) Unleavened bread shall be eaten seven days; and there shall no leavened bread be seen with thee, neither shall there be leaven seen with thee in all thy quarters. ^c13v7

[Exodus 13:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/13?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) ¶ And thou shalt shew thy son in that day, saying, This is done because of that which the LORD did unto me when I came forth out of Egypt. ^c13v8

[Exodus 13:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/13?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) And it shall be for a sign unto thee upon thine hand, and for a memorial between thine eyes, that the LORD's law may be in thy mouth: for with a strong hand hath the LORD brought thee out of Egypt. ^c13v9

[Exodus 13:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/13?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) Thou shalt therefore keep this ordinance in his season from year to year. ^c13v10

[Exodus 13:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/13?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) ¶ And it shall be when the LORD shall bring thee into the land of the Canaanites, as he sware unto thee and to thy fathers, and shall give it thee, ^c13v11

[Exodus 13:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/13?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) That thou shalt set apart unto the LORD all that openeth the matrix, and every firstling that cometh of a beast which thou hast; the males shall be the LORD's. ^c13v12

[Exodus 13:13](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/13?lang=eng&id=p13#p13) And every firstling of an ass thou shalt redeem with a lamb; and if thou wilt not redeem it, then thou shalt break his neck: and all the firstborn of man among thy children shalt thou redeem. ^c13v13

[Exodus 13:14](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/13?lang=eng&id=p14#p14) ¶ And it shall be when thy son asketh thee in time to come, saying, What is this?  that thou shalt say unto him, By strength of hand the LORD brought us out from Egypt, from the house of bondage: ^c13v14

[Exodus 13:15](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/13?lang=eng&id=p15#p15) And it came to pass, when Pharaoh would hardly let us go, that the LORD slew all the firstborn in the land of Egypt, both the firstborn of man, and the firstborn of beast: therefore I sacrifice to the LORD all that openeth the matrix, being males; but all the firstborn of my children I redeem. ^c13v15

[Exodus 13:16](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/13?lang=eng&id=p16#p16) And it shall be for a token upon thine hand, and for frontlets between thine eyes: for by strength of hand the LORD brought us forth out of Egypt. ^c13v16

[Exodus 13:17](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/13?lang=eng&id=p17#p17) ¶ And it came to pass, when Pharaoh had let the people go, that God led them not through the way of the land of the Philistines, although that was near; for God said, Lest peradventure the people repent when they see war, and they return to Egypt: ^c13v17

[Exodus 13:18](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/13?lang=eng&id=p18#p18) But God led the people about, through the way of the wilderness of the Red sea: and the children of Israel went up harnessed out of the land of Egypt. ^c13v18

[Exodus 13:19](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/13?lang=eng&id=p19#p19) And Moses took the bones of Joseph with him: for he had straitly sworn the children of Israel, saying, God will surely visit you; and ye shall carry up my bones away hence with you. ^c13v19

[Exodus 13:20](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/13?lang=eng&id=p20#p20) ¶ And they took their journey from Succoth, and encamped in Etham, in the edge of the wilderness. ^c13v20

[Exodus 13:21](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/13?lang=eng&id=p21#p21) And the LORD went before them by day in a pillar of a cloud, to lead them the way; and by night in a pillar of fire, to give them light; to go by day and night: ^c13v21

[Exodus 13:22](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/13?lang=eng&id=p22#p22) He took not away the pillar of the cloud by day, nor the pillar of fire by night, from before the people. ^c13v22

[Exodus 14:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) AND the LORD spake unto Moses, saying, ^c14v1

[Exodus 14:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) Speak unto the children of Israel, that they turn and encamp before Pi-hahiroth, between Migdol and the sea, over against Baal-zephon: before it shall ye encamp by the sea. ^c14v2

[Exodus 14:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) For Pharaoh will say of the children of Israel, They are entangled in the land, the wilderness hath shut them in. ^c14v3

[Exodus 14:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) And I will harden Pharaoh's heart, that he shall follow after them; and I will be honoured upon Pharaoh, and upon all his host; that the Egyptians may know that I am the LORD.  And they did so. ^c14v4

[Exodus 14:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) ¶ And it was told the king of Egypt that the people fled: and the heart of Pharaoh and of his servants was turned against the people, and they said, Why have we done this, that we have let Israel go from serving us? ^c14v5

[Exodus 14:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) And he made ready his chariot, and took his people with him: ^c14v6

[Exodus 14:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) And he took six hundred chosen chariots, and all the chariots of Egypt, and captains over every one of them. ^c14v7

[Exodus 14:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) And the LORD hardened the heart of Pharaoh king of Egypt, and he pursued after the children of Israel: and the children of Israel went out with an high hand. ^c14v8

[Exodus 14:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) But the Egyptians pursued after them, all the horses and chariots of Pharaoh, and his horsemen, and his army, and overtook them encamping by the sea, beside Pi-hahiroth, before Baal-zephon. ^c14v9

[Exodus 14:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) ¶ And when Pharaoh drew nigh, the children of Israel lifted up their eyes, and, behold, the Egyptians marched after them; and they were sore afraid: and the children of Israel cried out unto the LORD. ^c14v10

[Exodus 14:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) And they said unto Moses, Because there were no graves in Egypt, hast thou taken us away to die in the wilderness?  wherefore hast thou dealt thus with us, to carry us forth out of Egypt? ^c14v11

[Exodus 14:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) Is not this the word that we did tell thee in Egypt, saying, Let us alone, that we may serve the Egyptians?  For it had been better for us to serve the Egyptians, than that we should die in the wilderness. ^c14v12

[Exodus 14:13](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p13#p13) ¶ And Moses said unto the people, Fear ye not, stand still, and see the salvation of the LORD, which he will shew to you to day: for the Egyptians whom ye have seen to day, ye shall see them again no more for ever. ^c14v13

[Exodus 14:14](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p14#p14) The LORD shall fight for you, and ye shall hold your peace. ^c14v14

[Exodus 14:15](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p15#p15) ¶ And the LORD said unto Moses, Wherefore criest thou unto me? speak unto the children of Israel, that they go forward: ^c14v15

[Exodus 14:16](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p16#p16) But lift thou up thy rod, and stretch out thine hand over the sea, and divide it: and the children of Israel shall go on dry ground through the midst of the sea. ^c14v16

[Exodus 14:17](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p17#p17) And I, behold, I will harden the hearts of the Egyptians, and they shall follow them: and I will get me honour upon Pharaoh, and upon all his host, upon his chariots, and upon his horsemen. ^c14v17

[Exodus 14:18](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p18#p18) And the Egyptians shall know that I am the LORD, when I have gotten me honour upon Pharaoh, upon his chariots, and upon his horsemen. ^c14v18

[Exodus 14:19](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p19#p19) ¶ And the angel of God, which went before the camp of Israel, removed and went behind them; and the pillar of the cloud went from before their face, and stood behind them: ^c14v19

[Exodus 14:20](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p20#p20) And it came between the camp of the Egyptians and the camp of Israel; and it was a cloud and darkness to them, but it gave light by night to these: so that the one came not near the other all the night. ^c14v20

[Exodus 14:21](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p21#p21) And Moses stretched out his hand over the sea; and the LORD caused the sea to go back by a strong east wind all that night, and made the sea dry land, and the waters were divided. ^c14v21

[Exodus 14:22](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p22#p22) And the children of Israel went into the midst of the sea upon the dry ground: and the waters were a wall unto them on their right hand, and on their left. ^c14v22

[Exodus 14:23](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p23#p23) ¶ And the Egyptians pursued, and went in after them to the midst of the sea, even all Pharaoh's horses, his chariots, and his horsemen. ^c14v23

[Exodus 14:24](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p24#p24) And it came to pass, that in the morning watch the LORD looked unto the host of the Egyptians through the pillar of fire and of the cloud, and troubled the host of the Egyptians, ^c14v24

[Exodus 14:25](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p25#p25) And took off their chariot wheels, that they drave them heavily: so that the Egyptians said, Let us flee from the face of Israel; for the LORD fighteth for them against the Egyptians. ^c14v25

[Exodus 14:26](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p26#p26) ¶ And the LORD said unto Moses, Stretch out thine hand over the sea, that the waters may come again upon the Egyptians, upon their chariots, and upon their horsemen. ^c14v26

[Exodus 14:27](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p27#p27) And Moses stretched forth his hand over the sea, and the sea returned to his strength when the morning appeared; and the Egyptians fled against it; and the LORD overthrew the Egyptians in the midst of the sea. ^c14v27

[Exodus 14:28](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p28#p28) And the waters returned, and covered the chariots, and the horsemen, and all the host of Pharaoh that came into the sea after them; there remained not so much as one of them. ^c14v28

[Exodus 14:29](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p29#p29) But the children of Israel walked upon dry land in the midst of the sea; and the waters were a wall unto them on their right hand, and on their left. ^c14v29

[Exodus 14:30](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p30#p30) Thus the LORD saved Israel that day out of the hand of the Egyptians; and Israel saw the Egyptians dead upon the sea shore. ^c14v30

[Exodus 14:31](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/14?lang=eng&id=p31#p31) And Israel saw that great work which the LORD did upon the Egyptians: and the people feared the LORD, and believed the LORD, and his servant Moses. ^c14v31

[Exodus 15:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/15?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) THEN sang Moses and the children of Israel this song unto the LORD, and spake, saying, I will sing unto the LORD, for he hath triumphed gloriously: the horse and his rider hath he thrown into the sea. ^c15v1

[Exodus 15:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/15?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) The LORD is my strength and song, and he is become my salvation: he is my God, and I will prepare him an habitation; my father's God, and I will exalt him. ^c15v2

[Exodus 15:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/15?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) The LORD is a man of war: the LORD is his name. ^c15v3

[Exodus 15:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/15?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) Pharaoh's chariots and his host hath he cast into the sea: his chosen captains also are drowned in the Red sea. ^c15v4

[Exodus 15:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/15?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) The depths have covered them: they sank into the bottom as a stone. ^c15v5

[Exodus 15:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/15?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) Thy right hand, O LORD, is become glorious in power: thy right hand, O LORD, hath dashed in pieces the enemy. ^c15v6

[Exodus 15:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/15?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) And in the greatness of thine excellency thou hast overthrown them that rose up against thee: thou sentest forth thy wrath, which consumed them as stubble. ^c15v7

[Exodus 15:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/15?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) And with the blast of thy nostrils the waters were gathered together, the floods stood upright as an heap, and the depths were congealed in the heart of the sea. ^c15v8

[Exodus 15:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/15?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) The enemy said, I will pursue, I will overtake, I will divide the spoil; my lust shall be satisfied upon them; I will draw my sword, my hand shall destroy them. ^c15v9

[Exodus 15:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/15?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) Thou didst blow with thy wind, the sea covered them: they sank as lead in the mighty waters. ^c15v10

[Exodus 15:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/15?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) Who is like unto thee, O LORD, among the gods?  who is like thee, glorious in holiness, fearful in praises, doing wonders? ^c15v11

[Exodus 15:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/15?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) Thou stretchedst out thy right hand, the earth swallowed them. ^c15v12

[Exodus 15:13](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/15?lang=eng&id=p13#p13) Thou in thy mercy hast led forth the people which thou hast redeemed: thou hast guided them in thy strength unto thy holy habitation. ^c15v13

[Exodus 15:14](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/15?lang=eng&id=p14#p14) The people shall hear, and be afraid: sorrow shall take hold on the inhabitants of Palestina. ^c15v14

[Exodus 15:15](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/15?lang=eng&id=p15#p15) Then the dukes of Edom shall be amazed; the mighty men of Moab, trembling shall take hold upon them; all the inhabitants of Canaan shall melt away. ^c15v15

[Exodus 15:16](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/15?lang=eng&id=p16#p16) Fear and dread shall fall upon them; by the greatness of thine arm they shall be as still as a stone; till thy people pass over, O LORD, till the people pass over, which thou hast purchased. ^c15v16

[Exodus 15:17](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/15?lang=eng&id=p17#p17) Thou shalt bring them in, and plant them in the mountain of thine inheritance, in the place, O LORD, which thou hast made for thee to dwell in, in the Sanctuary, O Lord, which thy hands have established. ^c15v17

[Exodus 15:18](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/15?lang=eng&id=p18#p18) The LORD shall reign for ever and ever. ^c15v18

[Exodus 15:20](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/15?lang=eng&id=p20#p20) ¶ And Miriam the prophetess, the sister of Aaron, took a timbrel in her hand; and all the women went out after her with timbrels and with dances. ^c15v20

[Exodus 15:21](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/15?lang=eng&id=p21#p21) And Miriam answered them, Sing ye to the LORD, for he hath triumphed gloriously; the horse and his rider hath he thrown into the sea. ^c15v21

[Exodus 15:22](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/15?lang=eng&id=p22#p22) So Moses brought Israel from the Red sea, and they went out into the wilderness of Shur; and they went three days in the wilderness, and found no water. ^c15v22

[Exodus 15:23](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/15?lang=eng&id=p23#p23) ¶ And when they came to Marah, they could not drink of the waters of Marah, for they were bitter: therefore the name of it was called Marah. ^c15v23

[Exodus 15:26](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/15?lang=eng&id=p26#p26) And said, If thou wilt diligently hearken to the voice of the LORD thy God, and wilt do that which is right in his sight, and wilt give ear to his commandments, and keep all his statutes, I will put none of these diseases upon thee, which I have brought upon the Egyptians: for I am the LORD that healeth thee. ^c15v26

[Exodus 16:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) AND they took their journey from Elim, and all the congregation of the children of Israel came unto the wilderness of Sin, which is between Elim and Sinai, on the fifteenth day of the second month after their departing out of the land of Egypt. ^c16v1

[Exodus 16:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) And the whole congregation of the children of Israel murmured against Moses and Aaron in the wilderness: ^c16v2

[Exodus 16:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) And the children of Israel said unto them, Would to God we had died by the hand of the LORD in the land of Egypt, when we sat by the flesh pots, and when we did eat bread to the full; for ye have brought us forth into this wilderness, to kill this whole assembly with hunger. ^c16v3

[Exodus 16:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) ¶ Then said the LORD unto Moses, Behold, I will rain bread from heaven for you; and the people shall go out and gather a certain rate every day, that I may prove them, whether they will walk in my law, or no. ^c16v4

[Exodus 16:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) And it shall come to pass, that on the sixth day they shall prepare that which they bring in; and it shall be twice as much as they gather daily. ^c16v5

[Exodus 16:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) And Moses and Aaron said unto all the children of Israel, At even, then ye shall know that the LORD hath brought you out from the land of Egypt: ^c16v6

[Exodus 16:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) And in the morning, then ye shall see the glory of the LORD; for that he heareth your murmurings against the LORD: and what are we, that ye murmur against us? ^c16v7

[Exodus 16:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) And Moses said, This shall be, when the LORD shall give you in the evening flesh to eat, and in the morning bread to the full; for that the LORD heareth your murmurings which ye murmur against him: and what are we?  your murmurings are not against us, but against the LORD. ^c16v8

[Exodus 16:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) ¶ And Moses spake unto Aaron, Say unto all the congregation of the children of Israel, Come near before the LORD: for he hath heard your murmurings. ^c16v9

[Exodus 16:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) And it came to pass, as Aaron spake unto the whole congregation of the children of Israel, that they looked toward the wilderness, and, behold, the glory of the LORD appeared in the cloud. ^c16v10

[Exodus 16:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) ¶ And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying, ^c16v11

[Exodus 16:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) I have heard the murmurings of the children of Israel: speak unto them, saying, At even ye shall eat flesh, and in the morning ye shall be filled with bread; and ye shall know that I am the LORD your God. ^c16v12

[Exodus 16:13](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p13#p13) And it came to pass, that at even the quails came up, and covered the camp: and in the morning the dew lay round about the host. ^c16v13

[Exodus 16:14](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p14#p14) And when the dew that lay was gone up, behold, upon the face of the wilderness there lay a small round thing, as small as the hoar frost on the ground. ^c16v14

[Exodus 16:15](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p15#p15) And when the children of Israel saw it, they said one to another, It is manna: for they wist not what it was.  And Moses said unto them, This is the bread which the LORD hath given you to eat. ^c16v15

[Exodus 16:16](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p16#p16) ¶ This is the thing which the LORD hath commanded, Gather of it every man according to his eating, an omer for every man, according to the number of your persons; take ye every man for them which are in his tents. ^c16v16

[Exodus 16:17](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p17#p17) And the children of Israel did so, and gathered, some more, some less. ^c16v17

[Exodus 16:18](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p18#p18) And when they did mete it with an omer, he that gathered much had nothing over, and he that gathered little had no lack; they gathered every man according to his eating. ^c16v18

[Exodus 16:19](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p19#p19) And Moses said, Let no man leave of it till the morning. ^c16v19

[Exodus 16:20](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p20#p20) Notwithstanding they hearkened not unto Moses; but some of them left of it until the morning, and it bred worms, and stank: and Moses was wroth with them. ^c16v20

[Exodus 16:21](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p21#p21) And they gathered it every morning, every man according to his eating: and when the sun waxed hot, it melted. ^c16v21

[Exodus 16:22](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p22#p22) ¶ And it came to pass, that on the sixth day they gathered twice as much bread, two omers for one man: and all the rulers of the congregation came and told Moses. ^c16v22

[Exodus 16:23](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p23#p23) And he said unto them, This is that which the LORD hath said, To morrow is the rest of the holy sabbath unto the LORD: bake that which ye will bake to day, and seethe that ye will seethe; and that which remaineth over lay up for you to be kept until the morning. ^c16v23

[Exodus 16:24](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p24#p24) And they laid it up till the morning, as Moses bade: and it did not stink, neither was there any worm therein. ^c16v24

[Exodus 16:25](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p25#p25) And Moses said, Eat that to day; for to day is a sabbath unto the LORD: to day ye shall not find it in the field. ^c16v25

[Exodus 16:26](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p26#p26) Six days ye shall gather it; but on the seventh day, which is the sabbath, in it there shall be none. ^c16v26

[Exodus 16:27](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p27#p27) ¶ And it came to pass, that there went out some of the people on the seventh day for to gather, and they found none. ^c16v27

[Exodus 16:28](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p28#p28) And the LORD said unto Moses, How long refuse ye to keep my commandments and my laws? ^c16v28

[Exodus 16:29](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p29#p29) See, for that the LORD hath given you the sabbath, therefore he giveth you on the sixth day the bread of two days; abide ye every man in his place, let no man go out of his place on the seventh day. ^c16v29

[Exodus 16:30](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p30#p30) So the people rested on the seventh day. ^c16v30

[Exodus 16:31](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p31#p31) And the house of Israel called the name thereof Manna: and it was like coriander seed, white; and the taste of it was like wafers made with honey. ^c16v31

[Exodus 16:32](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p32#p32) ¶ And Moses said, This is the thing which the LORD commandeth, Fill an omer of it to be kept for your generations; that they may see the bread wherewith I have fed you in the wilderness, when I brought you forth from the land of Egypt. ^c16v32

[Exodus 16:33](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p33#p33) And Moses said unto Aaron, Take a pot, and put an omer full of manna therein, and lay it up before the LORD, to be kept for your generations. ^c16v33

[Exodus 16:34](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p34#p34) As the LORD commanded Moses, so Aaron laid it up before the Testimony, to be kept. ^c16v34

[Exodus 16:35](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p35#p35) And the children of Israel did eat manna forty years, until they came to a land inhabited; they did eat manna, until they came unto the borders of the land of Canaan. ^c16v35

[Exodus 16:36](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/16?lang=eng&id=p36#p36) Now an omer is the tenth part of an ephah. ^c16v36

[Exodus 17:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/17?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) AND all the congregation of the children of Israel journeyed from the wilderness of Sin, after their journeys, according to the commandment of the LORD, and pitched in Rephidim: and there was no water for the people to drink. ^c17v1

[Exodus 17:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/17?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) Wherefore the people did chide with Moses, and said, Give us water that we may drink.  And Moses said unto them, Why chide ye with me?  wherefore do ye tempt the LORD? ^c17v2

[Exodus 17:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/17?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) And the people thirsted there for water; and the people murmured against Moses, and said, Wherefore is this that thou hast brought us up out of Egypt, to kill us and our children and our cattle with thirst? ^c17v3

[Exodus 17:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/17?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) And Moses cried unto the LORD, saying, What shall I do unto this people?  they be almost ready to stone me. ^c17v4

[Exodus 17:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/17?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) And the LORD said unto Moses, Go on before the people, and take with thee of the elders of Israel; and thy rod, wherewith thou smotest the river, take in thine hand, and go. ^c17v5

[Exodus 17:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/17?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) Behold, I will stand before thee there upon the rock in Horeb; and thou shalt smite the rock, and there shall come water out of it, that the people may drink.  And Moses did so in the sight of the elders of Israel. ^c17v6

[Exodus 17:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/17?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) And he called the name of the place Massah, and Meribah, because of the chiding of the children of Israel, and because they tempted the LORD, saying, Is the LORD among us, or not? ^c17v7

[Exodus 17:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/17?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) ¶ Then came Amalek, and fought with Israel in Rephidim. ^c17v8

[Exodus 17:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/17?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) And Moses said unto Joshua, Choose us out men, and go out, fight with Amalek: to morrow I will stand on the top of the hill with the rod of God in mine hand. ^c17v9

[Exodus 17:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/17?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) So Joshua did as Moses had said to him, and fought with Amalek: and Moses, Aaron, and Hur went up to the top of the hill. ^c17v10

[Exodus 17:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/17?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) And it came to pass, when Moses held up his hand, that Israel prevailed: and when he let down his hand, Amalek prevailed. ^c17v11

[Exodus 17:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/17?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) But Moses' hands were heavy; and they took a stone, and put it under him, and he sat thereon; and Aaron and Hur stayed up his hands, the one on the one side, and the other on the other side; and his hands were steady until the going down of the sun. ^c17v12

[Exodus 17:13](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/17?lang=eng&id=p13#p13) And Joshua discomfited Amalek and his people with the edge of the sword. ^c17v13

[Exodus 17:14](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/17?lang=eng&id=p14#p14) And the LORD said unto Moses, Write this for a memorial in a book, and rehearse it in the ears of Joshua: for I will utterly put out the remembrance of Amalek from under heaven. ^c17v14

[Exodus 17:15](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/17?lang=eng&id=p15#p15) And Moses built an altar, and called the name of it Jehovah-nissi: ^c17v15

[Exodus 17:16](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/17?lang=eng&id=p16#p16) For he said, Because the LORD hath sworn that the LORD will have war with Amalek from generation to generation. ^c17v16

[Exodus 18:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) WHEN Jethro, the priest of Midian, Moses' father in law, heard of all that God had done for Moses, and for Israel his people, and that the LORD had brought Israel out of Egypt; ^c18v1

[Exodus 18:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) Then Jethro, Moses' father in law, took Zipporah, Moses' wife, after he had sent her back, ^c18v2

[Exodus 18:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) And her two sons; of which the name of the one was Gershom; for he said, I have been an alien in a strange land: ^c18v3

[Exodus 18:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) And the name of the other was Eliezer; for the God of my father, said he, was mine help, and delivered me from the sword of Pharaoh: ^c18v4

[Exodus 18:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) And Jethro, Moses' father in law, came with his sons and his wife unto Moses into the wilderness, where he encamped at the mount of God: ^c18v5

[Exodus 18:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) And he said unto Moses, I thy father in law Jethro am come unto thee, and thy wife, and her two sons with her. ^c18v6

[Exodus 18:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) ¶ And Moses went out to meet his father in law, and did obeisance, and kissed him; and they asked each other of their welfare; and they came into the tent. ^c18v7

[Exodus 18:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) And Moses told his father in law all that the LORD had done unto Pharaoh and to the Egyptians for Israel's sake, and all the travail that had come upon them by the way, and how the LORD delivered them. ^c18v8

[Exodus 18:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) And Jethro rejoiced for all the goodness which the LORD had done to Israel, whom he had delivered out of the hand of the Egyptians. ^c18v9

[Exodus 18:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) And Jethro said, Blessed be the LORD, who hath delivered you out of the hand of the Egyptians, and out of the hand of Pharaoh, who hath delivered the people from under the hand of the Egyptians. ^c18v10

[Exodus 18:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) Now I know that the LORD is greater than all gods: for in the thing wherein they dealt proudly he was above them. ^c18v11

[Exodus 18:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) And Jethro, Moses' father in law, took a burnt offering and sacrifices for God: and Aaron came, and all the elders of Israel, to eat bread with Moses' father in law before God. ^c18v12

[Exodus 18:13](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p13#p13) ¶ And it came to pass on the morrow, that Moses sat to judge the people: and the people stood by Moses from the morning unto the evening. ^c18v13

[Exodus 18:14](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p14#p14) And when Moses' father in law saw all that he did to the people, he said, What is this thing that thou doest to the people?  why sittest thou thyself alone, and all the people stand by thee from morning unto even? ^c18v14

[Exodus 18:15](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p15#p15) And Moses said unto his father in law, Because the people come unto me to enquire of God: ^c18v15

[Exodus 18:16](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p16#p16) When they have a matter, they come unto me; and I judge between one and another, and I do make them know the statutes of God, and his laws. ^c18v16

[Exodus 18:17](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p17#p17) And Moses' father in law said unto him, The thing that thou doest is not good. ^c18v17

[Exodus 18:18](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p18#p18) Thou wilt surely wear away, both thou, and this people that is with thee: for this thing is too heavy for thee; thou art not able to perform it thyself alone. ^c18v18

[Exodus 18:19](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p19#p19) Hearken now unto my voice, I will give thee counsel, and God shall be with thee: Be thou for the people to God-ward, that thou mayest bring the causes unto God: ^c18v19

[Exodus 18:20](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p20#p20) And thou shalt teach them ordinances and laws, and shalt shew them the way wherein they must walk, and the work that they must do. ^c18v20

[Exodus 18:21](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p21#p21) Moreover thou shalt provide out of all the people able men, such as fear God, men of truth, hating covetousness; and place such over them, to be rulers of thousands, and rulers of hundreds, rulers of fifties, and rulers of tens: ^c18v21

[Exodus 18:22](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p22#p22) And let them judge the people at all seasons: and it shall be, that every great matter they shall bring unto thee, but every small matter they shall judge: so shall it be easier for thyself, and they shall bear the burden with thee. ^c18v22

[Exodus 18:23](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p23#p23) If thou shalt do this thing, and God command thee so, then thou shalt be able to endure, and all this people shall also go to their place in peace. ^c18v23

[Exodus 18:24](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p24#p24) So Moses hearkened to the voice of his father in law, and did all that he had said. ^c18v24

[Exodus 18:25](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p25#p25) And Moses chose able men out of all Israel, and made them heads over the people, rulers of thousands, rulers of hundreds, rulers of fifties, and rulers of tens. ^c18v25

[Exodus 18:26](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p26#p26) And they judged the people at all seasons: the hard causes they brought unto Moses, but every small matter they judged themselves. ^c18v26

[Exodus 18:27](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/18?lang=eng&id=p27#p27) ¶ And Moses let his father in law depart; and he went his way into his own land. ^c18v27

[Exodus 19:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/19?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) IN the third month, when the children of Israel were gone forth out of the land of Egypt, the same day came they into the wilderness of Sinai. ^c19v1

[Exodus 19:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/19?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) For they were departed from Rephidim, and were come to the desert of Sinai, and had pitched in the wilderness; and there Israel camped before the mount. ^c19v2

[Exodus 19:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/19?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) And Moses went up unto God, and the LORD called unto him out of the mountain, saying, Thus shalt thou say to the house of Jacob, and tell the children of Israel; ^c19v3

[Exodus 19:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/19?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) Ye have seen what I did unto the Egyptians, and how I bare you on eagles' wings, and brought you unto myself. ^c19v4

[Exodus 19:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/19?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) Now therefore, if ye will obey my voice indeed, and keep my covenant, then ye shall be a peculiar treasure unto me above all people: for all the earth is mine: ^c19v5

[Exodus 19:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/19?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) And ye shall be unto me a kingdom of priests, and an holy nation.  These are the words which thou shalt speak unto the children of Israel. ^c19v6

[Exodus 19:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/19?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) ¶ And Moses came and called for the elders of the people, and laid before their faces all these words which the LORD commanded him. ^c19v7

[Exodus 19:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/19?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) And all the people answered together, and said, All that the LORD hath spoken we will do.  And Moses returned the words of the people unto the LORD. ^c19v8

[Exodus 19:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/19?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) And the LORD said unto Moses, Lo, I come unto thee in a thick cloud, that the people may hear when I speak with thee, and believe thee for ever.  And Moses told the words of the people unto the LORD. ^c19v9

[Exodus 19:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/19?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) ¶ And the LORD said unto Moses, Go unto the people, and sanctify them to day and to morrow, and let them wash their clothes, ^c19v10

[Exodus 19:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/19?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) And be ready against the third day: for the third day the LORD will come down in the sight of all the people upon mount Sinai. ^c19v11

[Exodus 19:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/19?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) And thou shalt set bounds unto the people round about, saying, Take heed to yourselves, that ye go not up into the mount, or touch the border of it: whosoever toucheth the mount shall be surely put to death: ^c19v12

[Exodus 19:13](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/19?lang=eng&id=p13#p13) There shall not an hand touch it, but he shall surely be stoned, or shot through; whether it be beast or man, it shall not live: when the trumpet soundeth long, they shall come up to the mount. ^c19v13

[Exodus 19:14](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/19?lang=eng&id=p14#p14) ¶ And Moses went down from the mount unto the people, and sanctified the people; and they washed their clothes. ^c19v14

[Exodus 19:15](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/19?lang=eng&id=p15#p15) And he said unto the people, Be ready against the third day: come not at your wives. ^c19v15

[Exodus 19:16](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/19?lang=eng&id=p16#p16) ¶ And it came to pass on the third day in the morning, that there were thunders and lightnings, and a thick cloud upon the mount, and the voice of the trumpet exceeding loud; so that all the people that was in the camp trembled. ^c19v16

[Exodus 19:17](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/19?lang=eng&id=p17#p17) And Moses brought forth the people out of the camp to meet with God; and they stood at the nether part of the mount. ^c19v17

[Exodus 19:18](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/19?lang=eng&id=p18#p18) And mount Sinai was altogether on a smoke, because the LORD descended upon it in fire: and the smoke thereof ascended as the smoke of a furnace, and the whole mount quaked greatly. ^c19v18

[Exodus 19:19](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/19?lang=eng&id=p19#p19) And when the voice of the trumpet sounded long, and waxed louder and louder, Moses spake, and God answered him by a voice. ^c19v19

[Exodus 19:20](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/19?lang=eng&id=p20#p20) And the LORD came down upon mount Sinai, on the top of the mount: and the LORD called Moses up to the top of the mount; and Moses went up. ^c19v20

[Exodus 19:21](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/19?lang=eng&id=p21#p21) And the LORD said unto Moses, Go down, charge the people, lest they break through unto the LORD to gaze, and many of them perish. ^c19v21

[Exodus 19:22](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/19?lang=eng&id=p22#p22) And let the priests also, which come near to the LORD, sanctify themselves, lest the LORD break forth upon them. ^c19v22

[Exodus 19:23](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/19?lang=eng&id=p23#p23) And Moses said unto the LORD, The people cannot come up to mount Sinai: for thou chargedst us, saying, Set bounds about the mount, and sanctify it. ^c19v23

[Exodus 19:24](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/19?lang=eng&id=p24#p24) And the LORD said unto him, Away, get thee down, and thou shalt come up, thou, and Aaron with thee: but let not the priests and the people break through to come up unto the LORD, lest he break forth upon them. ^c19v24

[Exodus 19:25](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/19?lang=eng&id=p25#p25) So Moses went down unto the people, and spake unto them. ^c19v25

[Exodus 20:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/20?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) AND God spake all these words, saying, ^c20v1

[Exodus 20:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/20?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) I am the LORD thy God, which have brought thee out of the land of Egypt, out of the house of bondage. ^c20v2

[Exodus 20:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/20?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) Thou shalt have no other gods before me. ^c20v3

[Exodus 20:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/20?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) Thou shalt not make unto thee any graven image, or any likeness of any thing that is in heaven above, or that is in the earth beneath, or that is in the water under the earth: ^c20v4

[Exodus 20:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/20?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) Thou shalt not bow down thyself to them, nor serve them: for I the LORD thy God am a jealous God, visiting the iniquity of the fathers upon the children unto the third and fourth generation of them that hate me; ^c20v5

[Exodus 20:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/20?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) And shewing mercy unto thousands of them that love me, and keep my commandments. ^c20v6

[Exodus 20:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/20?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) Thou shalt not take the name of the LORD thy God in vain; for the LORD will not hold him guiltless that taketh his name in vain. ^c20v7

[Exodus 20:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/20?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) Remember the sabbath day, to keep it holy. ^c20v8

[Exodus 20:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/20?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) Six days shalt thou labour, and do all thy work: ^c20v9

[Exodus 20:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/20?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) But the seventh day is the sabbath of the LORD thy God: in it thou shalt not do any work, thou, nor thy son, nor thy daughter, thy manservant, nor thy maidservant, nor thy cattle, nor thy stranger that is within thy gates: ^c20v10

[Exodus 20:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/20?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) For in six days the LORD made heaven and earth, the sea, and all that in them is, and rested the seventh day: wherefore the LORD blessed the sabbath day, and hallowed it. ^c20v11

[Exodus 20:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/20?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) ¶ Honour thy father and thy mother: that thy days may be long upon the land which the LORD thy God giveth thee. ^c20v12

[Exodus 20:13](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/20?lang=eng&id=p13#p13) Thou shalt not kill. ^c20v13

[Exodus 20:14](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/20?lang=eng&id=p14#p14) Thou shalt not commit adultery. ^c20v14

[Exodus 20:15](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/20?lang=eng&id=p15#p15) Thou shalt not steal. ^c20v15

[Exodus 20:16](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/20?lang=eng&id=p16#p16) Thou shalt not bear false witness against thy neighbour. ^c20v16

[Exodus 20:17](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/20?lang=eng&id=p17#p17) Thou shalt not covet thy neighbour's house, thou shalt not covet thy neighbour's wife, nor his manservant, nor his maidservant, nor his ox, nor his ass, nor any thing that is thy neighbour's. ^c20v17

[Exodus 20:18](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/20?lang=eng&id=p18#p18) ¶ And all the people saw the thunderings, and the lightnings, and the noise of the trumpet, and the mountain smoking: and when the people saw it, they removed, and stood afar off. ^c20v18

[Exodus 20:19](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/20?lang=eng&id=p19#p19) And they said unto Moses, Speak thou with us, and we will hear: but let not God speak with us, lest we die. ^c20v19

[Exodus 20:20](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/20?lang=eng&id=p20#p20) And Moses said unto the people, Fear not: for God is come to prove you, and that his fear may be before your faces, that ye sin not. ^c20v20

[Exodus 20:21](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/20?lang=eng&id=p21#p21) And the people stood afar off, and Moses drew near unto the thick darkness where God was. ^c20v21

[Exodus 20:22](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/20?lang=eng&id=p22#p22) ¶ And the LORD said unto Moses, Thus thou shalt say unto the children of Israel, Ye have seen that I have talked with you from heaven. ^c20v22

[Exodus 20:23](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/20?lang=eng&id=p23#p23) Ye shall not make with me gods of silver, neither shall ye make unto you gods of gold. ^c20v23

[Exodus 20:24](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/20?lang=eng&id=p24#p24) ¶ An altar of earth thou shalt make unto me, and shalt sacrifice thereon thy burnt offerings, and thy peace offerings, thy sheep, and thine oxen: in all places where I record my name I will come unto thee, and I will bless thee. ^c20v24

[Exodus 20:25](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/20?lang=eng&id=p25#p25) And if thou wilt make me an altar of stone, thou shalt not build it of hewn stone: for if thou lift up thy tool upon it, thou hast polluted it. ^c20v25

[Exodus 20:26](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/20?lang=eng&id=p26#p26) Neither shalt thou go up by steps unto mine altar, that thy nakedness be not discovered thereon. ^c20v26

[Exodus 21:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) NOW these are the judgments which thou shalt set before them. ^c21v1

[Exodus 21:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) If thou buy an Hebrew servant, six years he shall serve: and in the seventh he shall go out free for nothing. ^c21v2

[Exodus 21:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) If he came in by himself, he shall go out by himself: if he were married, then his wife shall go out with him. ^c21v3

[Exodus 21:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) If his master have given him a wife, and she have born him sons or daughters; the wife and her children shall be her master's, and he shall go out by himself. ^c21v4

[Exodus 21:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) And if the servant shall plainly say, I love my master, my wife, and my children; I will not go out free: ^c21v5

[Exodus 21:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) Then his master shall bring him unto the judges; he shall also bring him to the door, or unto the door post; and his master shall bore his ear through with an aul; and he shall serve him for ever. ^c21v6

[Exodus 21:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) ¶ And if a man sell his daughter to be a maidservant, she shall not go out as the menservants do. ^c21v7

[Exodus 21:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) If she please not her master, who hath betrothed her to himself, then shall he let her be redeemed: to sell her unto a strange nation he shall have no power, seeing he hath dealt deceitfully with her. ^c21v8

[Exodus 21:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) And if he have betrothed her unto his son, he shall deal with her after the manner of daughters. ^c21v9

[Exodus 21:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) If he take him another wife; her food, her raiment, and her duty of marriage, shall he not diminish. ^c21v10

[Exodus 21:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) And if he do not these three unto her, then shall she go out free without money. ^c21v11

[Exodus 21:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) ¶ He that smiteth a man, so that he die, shall be surely put to death. ^c21v12

[Exodus 21:13](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p13#p13) And if a man lie not in wait, but God deliver him into his hand; then I will appoint thee a place whither he shall flee. ^c21v13

[Exodus 21:14](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p14#p14) But if a man come presumptuously upon his neighbour, to slay him with guile; thou shalt take him from mine altar, that he may die. ^c21v14

[Exodus 21:15](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p15#p15) ¶ And he that smiteth his father, or his mother, shall be surely put to death. ^c21v15

[Exodus 21:16](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p16#p16) ¶ And he that stealeth a man, and selleth him, or if he be found in his hand, he shall surely be put to death. ^c21v16

[Exodus 21:17](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p17#p17) ¶ And he that curseth his father, or his mother, shall surely be put to death. ^c21v17

[Exodus 21:18](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p18#p18) ¶ And if men strive together, and one smite another with a stone, or with his fist, and he die not, but keepeth his bed: ^c21v18

[Exodus 21:19](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p19#p19) If he rise again, and walk abroad upon his staff, then shall he that smote him be quit: only he shall pay for the loss of his time, and shall cause him to be thoroughly healed. ^c21v19

[Exodus 21:20](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p20#p20) ¶ And if a man smite his servant, or his maid, with a rod, and he die under his hand; he shall be surely punished. ^c21v20

[Exodus 21:21](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p21#p21) Notwithstanding, if he continue a day or two, he shall not be punished: for he is his money. ^c21v21

[Exodus 21:22](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p22#p22) ¶ If men strive, and hurt a woman with child, so that her fruit depart from her, and yet no mischief follow: he shall be surely punished, according as the woman's husband will lay upon him; and he shall pay as the judges determine. ^c21v22

[Exodus 21:23](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p23#p23) And if any mischief follow, then thou shalt give life for life, ^c21v23

[Exodus 21:24](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p24#p24) Eye for eye, tooth for tooth, hand for hand, foot for foot, ^c21v24

[Exodus 21:25](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p25#p25) Burning for burning, wound for wound, stripe for stripe. ^c21v25

[Exodus 21:26](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p26#p26) ¶ And if a man smite the eye of his servant, or the eye of his maid, that it perish; he shall let him go free for his eye's sake. ^c21v26

[Exodus 21:27](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p27#p27) And if he smite out his manservant's tooth, or his maidservant's tooth; he shall let him go free for his tooth's sake. ^c21v27

[Exodus 21:28](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p28#p28) ¶ If an ox gore a man or a woman, that they die: then the ox shall be surely stoned, and his flesh shall not be eaten; but the owner of the ox shall be quit. ^c21v28

[Exodus 21:29](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p29#p29) But if the ox were wont to push with his horn in time past, and it hath been testified to his owner, and he hath not kept him in, but that he hath killed a man or a woman; the ox shall be stoned, and his owner also shall be put to death. ^c21v29

[Exodus 21:30](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p30#p30) If there be laid on him a sum of money, then he shall give for the ransom of his life whatsoever is laid upon him. ^c21v30

[Exodus 21:31](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p31#p31) Whether he have gored a son, or have gored a daughter, according to this judgment shall it be done unto him. ^c21v31

[Exodus 21:32](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p32#p32) If the ox shall push a manservant or a maidservant; he shall give unto their master thirty shekels of silver, and the ox shall be stoned. ^c21v32

[Exodus 21:33](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p33#p33) ¶ And if a man shall open a pit, or if a man shall dig a pit, and not cover it, and an ox or an ass fall therein; ^c21v33

[Exodus 21:34](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p34#p34) The owner of the pit shall make it good, and give money unto the owner of them; and the dead beast shall be his. ^c21v34

[Exodus 21:35](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p35#p35) ¶ And if one man's ox hurt another's, that he die; then they shall sell the live ox, and divide the money of it; and the dead ox also they shall divide. ^c21v35

[Exodus 21:36](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/21?lang=eng&id=p36#p36) Or if it be known that the ox hath used to push in time past, and his owner hath not kept him in; he shall surely pay ox for ox; and the dead shall be his own. ^c21v36

[Exodus 22:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) IF a man shall steal an ox, or a sheep, and kill it, or sell it; he shall restore five oxen for an ox, and four sheep for a sheep. ^c22v1

[Exodus 22:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) ¶ If a thief be found breaking up, and be smitten that he die, there shall no blood be shed for him. ^c22v2

[Exodus 22:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) If the sun be risen upon him, there shall be blood shed for him; for he should make full restitution; if he have nothing, then he shall be sold for his theft. ^c22v3

[Exodus 22:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) If the theft be certainly found in his hand alive, whether it be ox, or ass, or sheep; he shall restore double. ^c22v4

[Exodus 22:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) ¶ If a man shall cause a field or vineyard to be eaten, and shall put in his beast, and shall feed in another man's field; of the best of his own field, and of the best of his own vineyard, shall he make restitution. ^c22v5

[Exodus 22:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) ¶ If fire break out, and catch in thorns, so that the stacks of corn, or the standing corn, or the field, be consumed therewith; he that kindled the fire shall surely make restitution. ^c22v6

[Exodus 22:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) ¶ If a man shall deliver unto his neighbour money or stuff to keep, and it be stolen out of the man's house; if the thief be found, let him pay double. ^c22v7

[Exodus 22:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) If the thief be not found, then the master of the house shall be brought unto the judges, to see whether he have put his hand unto his neighbour's goods. ^c22v8

[Exodus 22:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) For all manner of trespass, whether it be for ox, for ass, for sheep, for raiment, or for any manner of lost thing, which another challengeth to be his, the cause of both parties shall come before the judges; and whom the judges shall condemn, he shall pay double unto his neighbour. ^c22v9

[Exodus 22:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) If a man deliver unto his neighbour an ass, or an ox, or a sheep, or any beast, to keep; and it die, or be hurt, or driven away, no man seeing it: ^c22v10

[Exodus 22:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) Then shall an oath of the LORD be between them both, that he hath not put his hand unto his neighbour's goods; and the owner of it shall accept thereof, and he shall not make it good. ^c22v11

[Exodus 22:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) And if it be stolen from him, he shall make restitution unto the owner thereof. ^c22v12

[Exodus 22:13](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p13#p13) If it be torn in pieces, then let him bring it for witness, and he shall not make good that which was torn. ^c22v13

[Exodus 22:14](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p14#p14) ¶ And if a man borrow ought of his neighbour, and it be hurt, or die, the owner thereof being not with it, he shall surely make it good. ^c22v14

[Exodus 22:15](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p15#p15) But if the owner thereof be with it, he shall not make it good: if it be an hired thing, it came for his hire. ^c22v15

[Exodus 22:16](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p16#p16) ¶ And if a man entice a maid that is not betrothed, and lie with her, he shall surely endow her to be his wife. ^c22v16

[Exodus 22:17](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p17#p17) If her father utterly refuse to give her unto him, he shall pay money according to the dowry of virgins. ^c22v17

[Exodus 22:18](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p18#p18) ¶ Thou shalt not suffer a witch to live. ^c22v18

[Exodus 22:19](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p19#p19) ¶ Whosoever lieth with a beast shall surely be put to death. ^c22v19

[Exodus 22:20](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p20#p20) ¶ He that sacrificeth unto any god, save unto the LORD only, he shall be utterly destroyed. ^c22v20

[Exodus 22:21](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p21#p21) ¶ Thou shalt neither vex a stranger, nor oppress him: for ye were strangers in the land of Egypt. ^c22v21

[Exodus 22:22](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p22#p22) ¶ Ye shall not afflict any widow, or fatherless child. ^c22v22

[Exodus 22:23](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p23#p23) If thou afflict them in any wise, and they cry at all unto me, I will surely hear their cry; ^c22v23

[Exodus 22:24](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p24#p24) And my wrath shall wax hot, and I will kill you with the sword; and your wives shall be widows, and your children fatherless. ^c22v24

[Exodus 22:25](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p25#p25) ¶ If thou lend money to any of my people that is poor by thee, thou shalt not be to him as an usurer, neither shalt thou lay upon him usury. ^c22v25

[Exodus 22:26](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p26#p26) If thou at all take thy neighbour's raiment to pledge, thou shalt deliver it unto him by that the sun goeth down: ^c22v26

[Exodus 22:27](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p27#p27) For that is his covering only, it is his raiment for his skin: wherein shall he sleep?  and it shall come to pass, when he crieth unto me, that I will hear; for I am gracious. ^c22v27

[Exodus 22:28](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p28#p28) ¶ Thou shalt not revile the gods, nor curse the ruler of thy people. ^c22v28

[Exodus 22:29](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p29#p29) ¶ Thou shalt not delay to offer the first of thy ripe fruits, and of thy liquors: the firstborn of thy sons shalt thou give unto me. ^c22v29

[Exodus 22:30](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p30#p30) Likewise shalt thou do with thine oxen, and with thy sheep: seven days it shall be with his dam; on the eighth day thou shalt give it me. ^c22v30

[Exodus 22:31](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/22?lang=eng&id=p31#p31) ¶ And ye shall be holy men unto me: neither shall ye eat any flesh that is torn of beasts in the field; ye shall cast it to the dogs. ^c22v31

[Exodus 23:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) THOU shalt not raise a false report: put not thine hand with the wicked to be an unrighteous witness. ^c23v1

[Exodus 23:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) ¶ Thou shalt not follow a multitude to do evil; neither shalt thou speak in a cause to decline after many to wrest judgment: ^c23v2

[Exodus 23:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) ¶ Neither shalt thou countenance a poor man in his cause. ^c23v3

[Exodus 23:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) ¶ If thou meet thine enemy's ox or his ass going astray, thou shalt surely bring it back to him again. ^c23v4

[Exodus 23:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) If thou see the ass of him that hateth thee lying under his burden, and wouldest forbear to help him, thou shalt surely help with him. ^c23v5

[Exodus 23:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) Thou shalt not wrest the judgment of thy poor in his cause. ^c23v6

[Exodus 23:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) Keep thee far from a false matter; and the innocent and righteous slay thou not: for I will not justify the wicked. ^c23v7

[Exodus 23:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) ¶ And thou shalt take no gift: for the gift blindeth the wise, and perverteth the words of the righteous. ^c23v8

[Exodus 23:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) ¶ Also thou shalt not oppress a stranger: for ye know the heart of a stranger, seeing ye were strangers in the land of Egypt. ^c23v9

[Exodus 23:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) And six years thou shalt sow thy land, and shalt gather in the fruits thereof: ^c23v10

[Exodus 23:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) But the seventh year thou shalt let it rest and lie still; that the poor of thy people may eat: and what they leave the beasts of the field shall eat.  In like manner thou shalt deal with thy vineyard, and with thy oliveyard. ^c23v11

[Exodus 23:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) Six days thou shalt do thy work, and on the seventh day thou shalt rest: that thine ox and thine ass may rest, and the son of thy handmaid, and the stranger, may be refreshed. ^c23v12

[Exodus 23:13](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p13#p13) And in all things that I have said unto you be circumspect: and make no mention of the name of other gods, neither let it be heard out of thy mouth. ^c23v13

[Exodus 23:14](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p14#p14) ¶ Three times thou shalt keep a feast unto me in the year. ^c23v14

[Exodus 23:15](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p15#p15) Thou shalt keep the feast of unleavened bread: (thou shalt eat unleavened bread seven days, as I commanded thee, in the time appointed of the month Abib; for in it thou camest out from Egypt: and none shall appear before me empty:) ^c23v15

[Exodus 23:16](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p16#p16) And the feast of harvest, the firstfruits of thy labours, which thou hast sown in the field: and the feast of ingathering, which is in the end of the year, when thou hast gathered in thy labours out of the field. ^c23v16

[Exodus 23:17](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p17#p17) Three times in the year all thy males shall appear before the Lord GOD. ^c23v17

[Exodus 23:18](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p18#p18) Thou shalt not offer the blood of my sacrifice with leavened bread; neither shall the fat of my sacrifice remain until the morning. ^c23v18

[Exodus 23:19](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p19#p19) The first of the firstfruits of thy land thou shalt bring into the house of the LORD thy God.  Thou shalt not seethe a kid in his mother's milk. ^c23v19

[Exodus 23:20](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p20#p20) ¶ Behold, I send an Angel before thee, to keep thee in the way, and to bring thee into the place which I have prepared. ^c23v20

[Exodus 23:21](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p21#p21) Beware of him, and obey his voice, provoke him not; for he will not pardon your transgressions: for my name is in him. ^c23v21

[Exodus 23:22](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p22#p22) But if thou shalt indeed obey his voice, and do all that I speak; then I will be an enemy unto thine enemies, and an adversary unto thine adversaries. ^c23v22

[Exodus 23:23](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p23#p23) For mine Angel shall go before thee, and bring thee in unto the Amorites, and the Hittites, and the Perizzites, and the Canaanites, and the Hivites, and the Jebusites: and I will cut them off. ^c23v23

[Exodus 23:24](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p24#p24) Thou shalt not bow down to their gods, nor serve them, nor do after their works: but thou shalt utterly overthrow them, and quite break down their images. ^c23v24

[Exodus 23:25](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p25#p25) And ye shall serve the LORD your God, and he shall bless thy bread, and thy water; and I will take sickness away from the midst of thee. ^c23v25

[Exodus 23:26](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p26#p26) ¶ There shall nothing cast their young, nor be barren, in thy land: the number of thy days I will fulfil. ^c23v26

[Exodus 23:27](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p27#p27) I will send my fear before thee, and will destroy all the people to whom thou shalt come, and I will make all thine enemies turn their backs unto thee. ^c23v27

[Exodus 23:28](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p28#p28) And I will send hornets before thee, which shall drive out the Hivite, the Canaanite, and the Hittite, from before thee. ^c23v28

[Exodus 23:29](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p29#p29) I will not drive them out from before thee in one year; lest the land become desolate, and the beast of the field multiply against thee. ^c23v29

[Exodus 23:30](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p30#p30) By little and little I will drive them out from before thee, until thou be increased, and inherit the land. ^c23v30

[Exodus 23:31](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p31#p31) And I will set thy bounds from the Red sea even unto the sea of the Philistines, and from the desert unto the river: for I will deliver the inhabitants of the land into your hand; and thou shalt drive them out before thee. ^c23v31

[Exodus 23:32](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p32#p32) Thou shalt make no covenant with them, nor with their gods. ^c23v32

[Exodus 23:33](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/23?lang=eng&id=p33#p33) They shall not dwell in thy land, lest they make thee sin against me: for if thou serve their gods, it will surely be a snare unto thee. ^c23v33

[Exodus 24:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/24?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) AND he said unto Moses, Come up unto the LORD, thou, and Aaron, Nadab, and Abihu, and seventy of the elders of Israel; and worship ye afar off. ^c24v1

[Exodus 24:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/24?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) And Moses alone shall come near the LORD: but they shall not come nigh; neither shall the people go up with him. ^c24v2

[Exodus 24:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/24?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) ¶ And Moses came and told the people all the words of the LORD, and all the judgments: and all the people answered with one voice, and said, All the words which the LORD hath said will we do. ^c24v3

[Exodus 24:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/24?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) And Moses wrote all the words of the LORD, and rose up early in the morning, and builded an altar under the hill, and twelve pillars, according to the twelve tribes of Israel. ^c24v4

[Exodus 24:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/24?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) And he sent young men of the children of Israel, which offered burnt offerings, and sacrificed peace offerings of oxen unto the LORD. ^c24v5

[Exodus 24:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/24?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) And Moses took half of the blood, and put it in basons; and half of the blood he sprinkled on the altar. ^c24v6

[Exodus 24:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/24?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) And he took the book of the covenant, and read in the audience of the people: and they said, All that the LORD hath said will we do, and be obedient. ^c24v7

[Exodus 24:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/24?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) And Moses took the blood, and sprinkled it on the people, and said, Behold the blood of the covenant, which the LORD hath made with you concerning all these words. ^c24v8

[Exodus 24:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/24?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) ¶ Then went up Moses, and Aaron, Nadab, and Abihu, and seventy of the elders of Israel: ^c24v9

[Exodus 24:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/24?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) And they saw the God of Israel: and there was under his feet as it were a paved work of a sapphire stone, and as it were the body of heaven in his clearness. ^c24v10

[Exodus 24:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/24?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) And upon the nobles of the children of Israel he laid not his hand: also they saw God, and did eat and drink. ^c24v11

[Exodus 24:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/24?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) ¶ And the LORD said unto Moses, Come up to me into the mount, and be there: and I will give thee tables of stone, and a law, and commandments which I have written; that thou mayest teach them. ^c24v12

[Exodus 24:13](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/24?lang=eng&id=p13#p13) And Moses rose up, and his minister Joshua: and Moses went up into the mount of God. ^c24v13

[Exodus 24:14](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/24?lang=eng&id=p14#p14) And he said unto the elders, Tarry ye here for us, until we come again unto you: and, behold, Aaron and Hur are with you: if any man have any matters to do, let him come unto them. ^c24v14

[Exodus 24:15](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/24?lang=eng&id=p15#p15) And Moses went up into the mount, and a cloud covered the mount. ^c24v15

[Exodus 24:16](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/24?lang=eng&id=p16#p16) And the glory of the LORD abode upon mount Sinai, and the cloud covered it six days: and the seventh day he called unto Moses out of the midst of the cloud. ^c24v16

[Exodus 24:17](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/24?lang=eng&id=p17#p17) And the sight of the glory of the LORD was like devouring fire on the top of the mount in the eyes of the children of Israel. ^c24v17
