[Exodus 33:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/33?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) AND the LORD said unto Moses, Depart, and go up hence, thou and the people which thou hast brought up out of the land of Egypt, unto the land which I sware unto Abraham, to Isaac, and to Jacob, saying, Unto thy seed will I give it: ^c33v1

[Exodus 33:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/33?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) And I will send an angel before thee; and I will drive out the Canaanite, the Amorite, and the Hittite, and the Perizzite, the Hivite, and the Jebusite: ^c33v2

[Exodus 33:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/33?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) Unto a land flowing with milk and honey: for I will not go up in the midst of thee; for thou art a stiffnecked people: lest I consume thee in the way. ^c33v3

[Exodus 33:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/33?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) ¶ And when the people heard these evil tidings, they mourned: and no man did put on him his ornaments. ^c33v4

[Exodus 33:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/33?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) For the LORD had said unto Moses, Say unto the children of Israel, Ye are a stiffnecked people: I will come up into the midst of thee in a moment, and consume thee: therefore now put off thy ornaments from thee, that I may know what to do unto thee. ^c33v5

[Exodus 33:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/33?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) And the children of Israel stripped themselves of their ornaments by the mount Horeb. ^c33v6

[Exodus 33:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/33?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) And Moses took the tabernacle, and pitched it without the camp, afar off from the camp, and called it the Tabernacle of the congregation.  And it came to pass, that every one which sought the LORD went out unto the tabernacle of the congregation, which was without the camp. ^c33v7

[Exodus 33:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/33?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) And it came to pass, when Moses went out unto the tabernacle, that all the people rose up, and stood every man at his tent door, and looked after Moses, until he was gone into the tabernacle. ^c33v8

[Exodus 33:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/33?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) And it came to pass, as Moses entered into the tabernacle, the cloudy pillar descended, and stood at the door of the tabernacle, and the LORD talked with Moses. ^c33v9

[Exodus 33:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/33?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) And all the people saw the cloudy pillar stand at the tabernacle door: and all the people rose up and worshipped, every man in his tent door. ^c33v10

[Exodus 33:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/33?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) And the LORD spake unto Moses face to face, as a man speaketh unto his friend.  And he turned again into the camp: but his servant Joshua, the son of Nun, a young man, departed not out of the tabernacle. ^c33v11

[Exodus 33:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/33?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) ¶ And Moses said unto the LORD, See, thou sayest unto me, Bring up this people: and thou hast not let me know whom thou wilt send with me.  Yet thou hast said, I know thee by name, and thou hast also found grace in my sight. ^c33v12

[Exodus 33:13](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/33?lang=eng&id=p13#p13) Now therefore, I pray thee, if I have found grace in thy sight, shew me now thy way, that I may know thee, that I may find grace in thy sight: and consider that this nation is thy people. ^c33v13

[Exodus 33:14](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/33?lang=eng&id=p14#p14) And he said, My presence shall go with thee, and I will give thee rest. ^c33v14

[Exodus 33:15](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/33?lang=eng&id=p15#p15) And he said unto him, If thy presence go not with me, carry us not up hence. ^c33v15

[Exodus 33:16](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/33?lang=eng&id=p16#p16) For wherein shall it be known here that I and thy people have found grace in thy sight?  is it not in that thou goest with us?  so shall we be separated, I and thy people, from all the people that are upon the face of the earth. ^c33v16

[Exodus 33:17](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/33?lang=eng&id=p17#p17) And the LORD said unto Moses, I will do this thing also that thou hast spoken: for thou hast found grace in my sight, and I know thee by name. ^c33v17

[Exodus 33:18](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/33?lang=eng&id=p18#p18) And he said, I beseech thee, shew me thy glory. ^c33v18

[Exodus 33:19](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/33?lang=eng&id=p19#p19) And he said, I will make all my goodness pass before thee, and I will proclaim the name of the LORD before thee; and will be gracious to whom I will be gracious, and will shew mercy on whom I will shew mercy. ^c33v19

[Exodus 33:20](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/33?lang=eng&id=p20#p20) And he said, Thou canst not see my face: for there shall no man see me, and live. ^c33v20

[Exodus 33:21](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/33?lang=eng&id=p21#p21) And the LORD said, Behold, there is a place by me, and thou shalt stand upon a rock: ^c33v21

[Exodus 33:22](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/33?lang=eng&id=p22#p22) And it shall come to pass, while my glory passeth by, that I will put thee in a clift of the rock, and will cover thee with my hand while I pass by: ^c33v22

[Exodus 33:23](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/33?lang=eng&id=p23#p23) And I will take away mine hand, and thou shalt see my back parts: but my face shall not be seen. ^c33v23

[Exodus 34:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) AND the LORD said unto Moses, Hew thee two tables of stone like unto the first: and I will write upon these tables the words that were in the first tables, which thou brakest. ^c34v1

[Exodus 34:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) And be ready in the morning, and come up in the morning unto mount Sinai, and present thyself there to me in the top of the mount. ^c34v2

[Exodus 34:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) And no man shall come up with thee, neither let any man be seen throughout all the mount; neither let the flocks nor herds feed before that mount. ^c34v3

[Exodus 34:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) ¶ And he hewed two tables of stone like unto the first; and Moses rose up early in the morning, and went up unto mount Sinai, as the LORD had commanded him, and took in his hand the two tables of stone. ^c34v4

[Exodus 34:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) And the LORD descended in the cloud, and stood with him there, and proclaimed the name of the LORD. ^c34v5

[Exodus 34:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) And the LORD passed by before him, and proclaimed, The LORD, The LORD God, merciful and gracious, longsuffering, and abundant in goodness and truth, ^c34v6

[Exodus 34:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) Keeping mercy for thousands, forgiving iniquity and transgression and sin, and that will by no means clear the guilty; visiting the iniquity of the fathers upon the children, and upon the children's children, unto the third and to the fourth generation. ^c34v7

[Exodus 34:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) And Moses made haste, and bowed his head toward the earth, and worshipped. ^c34v8

[Exodus 34:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) And he said, If now I have found grace in thy sight, O Lord, let my Lord, I pray thee, go among us; for it is a stiffnecked people; and pardon our iniquity and our sin, and take us for thine inheritance. ^c34v9

[Exodus 34:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) ¶ And he said, Behold, I make a covenant: before all thy people I will do marvels, such as have not been done in all the earth, nor in any nation: and all the people among which thou art shall see the work of the LORD: for it is a terrible thing that I will do with thee. ^c34v10

[Exodus 34:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) Observe thou that which I command thee this day: behold, I drive out before thee the Amorite, and the Canaanite, and the Hittite, and the Perizzite, and the Hivite, and the Jebusite. ^c34v11

[Exodus 34:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) Take heed to thyself, lest thou make a covenant with the inhabitants of the land whither thou goest, lest it be for a snare in the midst of thee: ^c34v12

[Exodus 34:13](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p13#p13) But ye shall destroy their altars, break their images, and cut down their groves: ^c34v13

[Exodus 34:14](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p14#p14) For thou shalt worship no other god: for the LORD, whose name is Jealous, is a jealous God: ^c34v14

[Exodus 34:15](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p15#p15) Lest thou make a covenant with the inhabitants of the land, and they go a whoring after their gods, and do sacrifice unto their gods, and one call thee, and thou eat of his sacrifice; ^c34v15

[Exodus 34:16](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p16#p16) And thou take of their daughters unto thy sons, and their daughters go a whoring after their gods, and make thy sons go a whoring after their gods. ^c34v16

[Exodus 34:17](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p17#p17) Thou shalt make thee no molten gods. ^c34v17

[Exodus 34:18](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p18#p18) ¶ The feast of unleavened bread shalt thou keep.  Seven days thou shalt eat unleavened bread, as I commanded thee, in the time of the month Abib: for in the month Abib thou camest out from Egypt. ^c34v18

[Exodus 34:19](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p19#p19) All that openeth the matrix is mine; and every firstling among thy cattle, whether ox or sheep, that is male. ^c34v19

[Exodus 34:20](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p20#p20) But the firstling of an ass thou shalt redeem with a lamb: and if thou redeem him not, then shalt thou break his neck.  All the firstborn of thy sons thou shalt redeem.  And none shall appear before me empty. ^c34v20

[Exodus 34:21](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p21#p21) ¶ Six days thou shalt work, but on the seventh day thou shalt rest: in earing time and in harvest thou shalt rest. ^c34v21

[Exodus 34:22](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p22#p22) ¶ And thou shalt observe the feast of weeks, of the firstfruits of wheat harvest, and the feast of ingathering at the year's end. ^c34v22

[Exodus 34:23](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p23#p23) ¶ Thrice in the year shall all your men children appear before the Lord GOD, the God of Israel. ^c34v23

[Exodus 34:24](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p24#p24) For I will cast out the nations before thee, and enlarge thy borders: neither shall any man desire thy land, when thou shalt go up to appear before the LORD thy God thrice in the year. ^c34v24

[Exodus 34:25](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p25#p25) Thou shalt not offer the blood of my sacrifice with leaven; neither shall the sacrifice of the feast of the passover be left unto the morning. ^c34v25

[Exodus 34:26](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p26#p26) The first of the firstfruits of thy land thou shalt bring unto the house of the LORD thy God.  Thou shalt not seethe a kid in his mother's milk. ^c34v26

[Exodus 34:27](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p27#p27) And the LORD said unto Moses, Write thou these words: for after the tenor of these words I have made a covenant with thee and with Israel. ^c34v27

[Exodus 34:28](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p28#p28) And he was there with the LORD forty days and forty nights; he did neither eat bread, nor drink water.  And he wrote upon the tables the words of the covenant, the ten commandments. ^c34v28

[Exodus 34:29](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p29#p29) ¶ And it came to pass, when Moses came down from mount Sinai with the two tables of testimony in Moses' hand, when he came down from the mount, that Moses wist not that the skin of his face shone while he talked with him. ^c34v29

[Exodus 34:30](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p30#p30) And when Aaron and all the children of Israel saw Moses, behold, the skin of his face shone; and they were afraid to come nigh him. ^c34v30

[Exodus 34:31](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p31#p31) And Moses called unto them; and Aaron and all the rulers of the congregation returned unto him: and Moses talked with them. ^c34v31

[Exodus 34:32](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p32#p32) And afterward all the children of Israel came nigh: and he gave them in commandment all that the LORD had spoken with him in mount Sinai. ^c34v32

[Exodus 34:33](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p33#p33) And till Moses had done speaking with them, he put a vail on his face. ^c34v33

[Exodus 34:34](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p34#p34) But when Moses went in before the LORD to speak with him, he took the vail off, until he came out.  And he came out, and spake unto the children of Israel that which he was commanded. ^c34v34

[Exodus 34:35](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/34?lang=eng&id=p35#p35) And the children of Israel saw the face of Moses, that the skin of Moses' face shone: and Moses put the vail upon his face again, until he went in to speak with him. ^c34v35

[Exodus 35:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/35?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) AND Moses gathered all the congregation of the children of Israel together, and said unto them, These are the words which the LORD hath commanded, that ye should do them. ^c35v1

[Exodus 35:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/35?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) Ye shall kindle no fire throughout your habitations upon the sabbath day. ^c35v3

[Exodus 35:24](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/35?lang=eng&id=p24#p24) Every one that did offer an offering of silver and brass brought the LORD's offering: and every man, with whom was found shittim wood for any work of the service, brought it. ^c35v24

[Exodus 35:28](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/35?lang=eng&id=p28#p28) And spice, and oil for the light, and for the anointing oil, and for the sweet incense. ^c35v28

[Exodus 35:30](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/35?lang=eng&id=p30#p30) ¶ And Moses said unto the children of Israel, See, the LORD hath called by name Bezaleel the son of Uri, the son of Hur, of the tribe of Judah; ^c35v30

[Exodus 35:31](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/35?lang=eng&id=p31#p31) And he hath filled him with the spirit of God, in wisdom, in understanding, and in knowledge, and in all manner of workmanship; ^c35v31

[Exodus 35:32](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/35?lang=eng&id=p32#p32) And to devise curious works, to work in gold, and in silver, and in brass, ^c35v32

[Exodus 35:34](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/35?lang=eng&id=p34#p34) And he hath put in his heart that he may teach, both he, and Aholiab, the son of Ahisamach, of the tribe of Dan. ^c35v34

[Exodus 35:35](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/35?lang=eng&id=p35#p35) Them hath he filled with wisdom of heart, to work all manner of work, of the engraver, and of the cunning workman, and of the embroiderer, in blue, and in purple, in scarlet, and in fine linen, and of the weaver, even of them that do any work, and of those that devise cunning work. ^c35v35

[Exodus 36:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) THEN wrought Bezaleel and Aholiab, and every wise hearted man, in whom the LORD put wisdom and understanding to know how to work all manner of work for the service of the sanctuary, according to all that the LORD had commanded. ^c36v1

[Exodus 36:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) And Moses called Bezaleel and Aholiab, and every wise hearted man, in whose heart the LORD had put wisdom, even every one whose heart stirred him up to come unto the work to do it: ^c36v2

[Exodus 36:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) And they received of Moses all the offering, which the children of Israel had brought for the work of the service of the sanctuary, to make it withal.  And they brought yet unto him free offerings every morning. ^c36v3

[Exodus 36:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) And all the wise men, that wrought all the work of the sanctuary, came every man from his work which they made; ^c36v4

[Exodus 36:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) ¶ And they spake unto Moses, saying, The people bring much more than enough for the service of the work, which the LORD commanded to make. ^c36v5

[Exodus 36:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) And Moses gave commandment, and they caused it to be proclaimed throughout the camp, saying, Let neither man nor woman make any more work for the offering of the sanctuary.  So the people were restrained from bringing. ^c36v6

[Exodus 36:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) For the stuff they had was sufficient for all the work to make it, and too much. ^c36v7

[Exodus 36:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) ¶ And every wise hearted man among them that wrought the work of the tabernacle made ten curtains of fine twined linen, and blue, and purple, and scarlet: with cherubims of cunning work made he them. ^c36v8

[Exodus 36:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) The length of one curtain was twenty and eight cubits, and the breadth of one curtain four cubits: the curtains were all of one size. ^c36v9

[Exodus 36:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) And he coupled the five curtains one unto another: and the other five curtains he coupled one unto another. ^c36v10

[Exodus 36:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) And he made loops of blue on the edge of one curtain from the selvedge in the coupling: likewise he made in the uttermost side of another curtain, in the coupling of the second. ^c36v11

[Exodus 36:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) Fifty loops made he in one curtain, and fifty loops made he in the edge of the curtain which was in the coupling of the second: the loops held one curtain to another. ^c36v12

[Exodus 36:13](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p13#p13) And he made fifty taches of gold, and coupled the curtains one unto another with the taches: so it became one tabernacle. ^c36v13

[Exodus 36:14](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p14#p14) ¶ And he made curtains of goats' hair for the tent over the tabernacle: eleven curtains he made them. ^c36v14

[Exodus 36:15](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p15#p15) The length of one curtain was thirty cubits, and four cubits was the breadth of one curtain: the eleven curtains were of one size. ^c36v15

[Exodus 36:16](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p16#p16) And he coupled five curtains by themselves, and six curtains by themselves. ^c36v16

[Exodus 36:17](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p17#p17) And he made fifty loops upon the uttermost edge of the curtain in the coupling, and fifty loops made he upon the edge of the curtain which coupleth the second. ^c36v17

[Exodus 36:18](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p18#p18) And he made fifty taches of brass to couple the tent together, that it might be one. ^c36v18

[Exodus 36:19](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p19#p19) And he made a covering for the tent of rams' skins dyed red, and a covering of badgers' skins above that. ^c36v19

[Exodus 36:20](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p20#p20) ¶ And he made boards for the tabernacle of shittim wood, standing up. ^c36v20

[Exodus 36:21](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p21#p21) The length of a board was ten cubits, and the breadth of a board one cubit and a half. ^c36v21

[Exodus 36:22](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p22#p22) One board had two tenons, equally distant one from another: thus did he make for all the boards of the tabernacle. ^c36v22

[Exodus 36:23](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p23#p23) And he made boards for the tabernacle; twenty boards for the south side southward: ^c36v23

[Exodus 36:24](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p24#p24) And forty sockets of silver he made under the twenty boards; two sockets under one board for his two tenons, and two sockets under another board for his two tenons. ^c36v24

[Exodus 36:25](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p25#p25) And for the other side of the tabernacle, which is toward the north corner, he made twenty boards, ^c36v25

[Exodus 36:26](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p26#p26) And their forty sockets of silver; two sockets under one board, and two sockets under another board. ^c36v26

[Exodus 36:27](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p27#p27) And for the sides of the tabernacle westward he made six boards. ^c36v27

[Exodus 36:28](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p28#p28) And two boards made he for the corners of the tabernacle in the two sides. ^c36v28

[Exodus 36:29](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p29#p29) And they were coupled beneath, and coupled together at the head thereof, to one ring: thus he did to both of them in both the corners. ^c36v29

[Exodus 36:30](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p30#p30) And there were eight boards; and their sockets were sixteen sockets of silver, under every board two sockets. ^c36v30

[Exodus 36:31](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p31#p31) ¶ And he made bars of shittim wood; five for the boards of the one side of the tabernacle, ^c36v31

[Exodus 36:32](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p32#p32) And five bars for the boards of the other side of the tabernacle, and five bars for the boards of the tabernacle for the sides westward. ^c36v32

[Exodus 36:33](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p33#p33) And he made the middle bar to shoot through the boards from the one end to the other. ^c36v33

[Exodus 36:34](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p34#p34) And he overlaid the boards with gold, and made their rings of gold to be places for the bars, and overlaid the bars with gold. ^c36v34

[Exodus 36:35](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p35#p35) ¶ And he made a vail of blue, and purple, and scarlet, and fine twined linen: with cherubims made he it of cunning work. ^c36v35

[Exodus 36:36](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p36#p36) And he made thereunto four pillars of shittim wood, and overlaid them with gold: their hooks were of gold; and he cast for them four sockets of silver. ^c36v36

[Exodus 36:37](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p37#p37) ¶ And he made an hanging for the tabernacle door of blue, and purple, and scarlet, and fine twined linen, of needlework; ^c36v37

[Exodus 36:38](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/36?lang=eng&id=p38#p38) And the five pillars of it with their hooks: and he overlaid their chapiters and their fillets with gold: but their five sockets were of brass. ^c36v38

[Exodus 37:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/37?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) AND Bezaleel made the ark of shittim wood: two cubits and a half was the length of it, and a cubit and a half the breadth of it, and a cubit and a half the height of it: ^c37v1

[Exodus 37:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/37?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) And he overlaid it with pure gold within and without, and made a crown of gold to it round about. ^c37v2

[Exodus 37:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/37?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) And he cast for it four rings of gold, to be set by the four corners of it; even two rings upon the one side of it, and two rings upon the other side of it. ^c37v3

[Exodus 37:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/37?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) And he made staves of shittim wood, and overlaid them with gold. ^c37v4

[Exodus 37:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/37?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) And he put the staves into the rings by the sides of the ark, to bear the ark. ^c37v5

[Exodus 37:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/37?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) ¶ And he made the mercy seat of pure gold: two cubits and a half was the length thereof, and one cubit and a half the breadth thereof. ^c37v6

[Exodus 37:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/37?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) And he made two cherubims of gold, beaten out of one piece made he them, on the two ends of the mercy seat; ^c37v7

[Exodus 37:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/37?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) One cherub on the end on this side, and another cherub on the other end on that side: out of the mercy seat made he the cherubims on the two ends thereof. ^c37v8

[Exodus 37:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/37?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) And the cherubims spread out their wings on high, and covered with their wings over the mercy seat, with their faces one to another; even to the mercy seatward were the faces of the cherubims. ^c37v9

[Exodus 37:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/37?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) ¶ And he made the table of shittim wood: two cubits was the length thereof, and a cubit the breadth thereof, and a cubit and a half the height thereof: ^c37v10

[Exodus 37:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/37?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) And he overlaid it with pure gold, and made thereunto a crown of gold round about. ^c37v11

[Exodus 37:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/37?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) Also he made thereunto a border of an handbreadth round about; and made a crown of gold for the border thereof round about. ^c37v12

[Exodus 37:13](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/37?lang=eng&id=p13#p13) And he cast for it four rings of gold, and put the rings upon the four corners that were in the four feet thereof. ^c37v13

[Exodus 37:14](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/37?lang=eng&id=p14#p14) Over against the border were the rings, the places for the staves to bear the table. ^c37v14

[Exodus 37:15](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/37?lang=eng&id=p15#p15) And he made the staves of shittim wood, and overlaid them with gold, to bear the table. ^c37v15

[Exodus 37:16](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/37?lang=eng&id=p16#p16) And he made the vessels which were upon the table, his dishes, and his spoons, and his bowls, and his covers to cover withal, of pure gold. ^c37v16

[Exodus 37:17](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/37?lang=eng&id=p17#p17) ¶ And he made the candlestick of pure gold: of beaten work made he the candlestick; his shaft, and his branch, his bowls, his knops, and his flowers, were of the same: ^c37v17

[Exodus 37:18](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/37?lang=eng&id=p18#p18) And six branches going out of the sides thereof; three branches of the candlestick out of the one side thereof, and three branches of the candlestick out of the other side thereof: ^c37v18

[Exodus 37:19](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/37?lang=eng&id=p19#p19) Three bowls made after the fashion of almonds in one branch, a knop and a flower; and three bowls made like almonds in another branch, a knop and a flower: so throughout the six branches going out of the candlestick. ^c37v19

[Exodus 37:20](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/37?lang=eng&id=p20#p20) And in the candlestick were four bowls made like almonds, his knops, and his flowers: ^c37v20

[Exodus 37:21](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/37?lang=eng&id=p21#p21) And a knop under two branches of the same, and a knop under two branches of the same, and a knop under two branches of the same, according to the six branches going out of it. ^c37v21

[Exodus 37:22](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/37?lang=eng&id=p22#p22) Their knops and their branches were of the same: all of it was one beaten work of pure gold. ^c37v22

[Exodus 37:23](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/37?lang=eng&id=p23#p23) And he made his seven lamps, and his snuffers, and his snuffdishes, of pure gold. ^c37v23

[Exodus 37:24](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/37?lang=eng&id=p24#p24) Of a talent of pure gold made he it, and all the vessels thereof. ^c37v24

[Exodus 37:26](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/37?lang=eng&id=p26#p26) And he overlaid it with pure gold, both the top of it, and the sides thereof round about, and the horns of it: also he made unto it a crown of gold round about. ^c37v26

[Exodus 38:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/38?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) AND he made the altar of burnt offering of shittim wood: five cubits was the length thereof, and five cubits the breadth thereof; it was foursquare; and three cubits the height thereof. ^c38v1

[Exodus 38:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/38?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) And he made the horns thereof on the four corners of it; the horns thereof were of the same: and he overlaid it with brass. ^c38v2

[Exodus 38:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/38?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) And he made for the altar a brasen grate of network under the compass thereof beneath unto the midst of it. ^c38v4

[Exodus 38:18](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/38?lang=eng&id=p18#p18) And the hanging for the gate of the court was needlework, of blue, and purple, and scarlet, and fine twined linen: and twenty cubits was the length, and the height in the breadth was five cubits, answerable to the hangings of the court. ^c38v18

[Exodus 40:1](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p1#p1) AND the LORD spake unto Moses, saying, ^c40v1

[Exodus 40:2](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p2#p2) On the first day of the first month shalt thou set up the tabernacle of the tent of the congregation. ^c40v2

[Exodus 40:3](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p3#p3) And thou shalt put therein the ark of the testimony, and cover the ark with the vail. ^c40v3

[Exodus 40:4](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p4#p4) And thou shalt bring in the table, and set in order the things that are to be set in order upon it; and thou shalt bring in the candlestick, and light the lamps thereof. ^c40v4

[Exodus 40:5](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p5#p5) And thou shalt set the altar of gold for the incense before the ark of the testimony, and put the hanging of the door to the tabernacle. ^c40v5

[Exodus 40:6](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p6#p6) And thou shalt set the altar of the burnt offering before the door of the tabernacle of the tent of the congregation. ^c40v6

[Exodus 40:7](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p7#p7) And thou shalt set the laver between the tent of the congregation and the altar, and shalt put water therein. ^c40v7

[Exodus 40:8](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p8#p8) And thou shalt set up the court round about, and hang up the hanging at the court gate. ^c40v8

[Exodus 40:9](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p9#p9) And thou shalt take the anointing oil, and anoint the tabernacle, and all that is therein, and shalt hallow it, and all the vessels thereof: and it shall be holy. ^c40v9

[Exodus 40:10](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p10#p10) And thou shalt anoint the altar of the burnt offering, and all his vessels, and sanctify the altar: and it shall be an altar most holy. ^c40v10

[Exodus 40:11](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p11#p11) And thou shalt anoint the laver and his foot, and sanctify it. ^c40v11

[Exodus 40:12](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p12#p12) And thou shalt bring Aaron and his sons unto the door of the tabernacle of the congregation, and wash them with water. ^c40v12

[Exodus 40:13](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p13#p13) And thou shalt put upon Aaron the holy garments, and anoint him, and sanctify him; that he may minister unto me in the priest's office. ^c40v13

[Exodus 40:14](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p14#p14) And thou shalt bring his sons, and clothe them with coats: ^c40v14

[Exodus 40:15](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p15#p15) And thou shalt anoint them, as thou didst anoint their father, that they may minister unto me in the priest's office: for their anointing shall surely be an everlasting priesthood throughout their generations. ^c40v15

[Exodus 40:16](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p16#p16) Thus did Moses: according to all that the LORD commanded him, so did he. ^c40v16

[Exodus 40:17](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p17#p17) ¶ And it came to pass in the first month in the second year, on the first day of the month, that the tabernacle was reared up. ^c40v17

[Exodus 40:18](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p18#p18) And Moses reared up the tabernacle, and fastened his sockets, and set up the boards thereof, and put in the bars thereof, and reared up his pillars. ^c40v18

[Exodus 40:19](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p19#p19) And he spread abroad the tent over the tabernacle, and put the covering of the tent above upon it; as the LORD commanded Moses. ^c40v19

[Exodus 40:20](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p20#p20) ¶ And he took and put the testimony into the ark, and set the staves on the ark, and put the mercy seat above upon the ark: ^c40v20

[Exodus 40:21](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p21#p21) And he brought the ark into the tabernacle, and set up the vail of the covering, and covered the ark of the testimony; as the LORD commanded Moses. ^c40v21

[Exodus 40:22](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p22#p22) ¶ And he put the table in the tent of the congregation, upon the side of the tabernacle northward, without the vail. ^c40v22

[Exodus 40:23](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p23#p23) And he set the bread in order upon it before the LORD; as the LORD had commanded Moses. ^c40v23

[Exodus 40:24](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p24#p24) ¶ And he put the candlestick in the tent of the congregation, over against the table, on the side of the tabernacle southward. ^c40v24

[Exodus 40:25](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p25#p25) And he lighted the lamps before the LORD; as the LORD commanded Moses. ^c40v25

[Exodus 40:26](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p26#p26) ¶ And he put the golden altar in the tent of the congregation before the vail: ^c40v26

[Exodus 40:27](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p27#p27) And he burnt sweet incense thereon; as the LORD commanded Moses. ^c40v27

[Exodus 40:28](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p28#p28) ¶ And he set up the hanging at the door of the tabernacle. ^c40v28

[Exodus 40:29](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p29#p29) And he put the altar of burnt offering by the door of the tabernacle of the tent of the congregation, and offered upon it the burnt offering and the meat offering; as the LORD commanded Moses. ^c40v29

[Exodus 40:30](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p30#p30) ¶ And he set the laver between the tent of the congregation and the altar, and put water there, to wash withal. ^c40v30

[Exodus 40:31](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p31#p31) And Moses and Aaron and his sons washed their hands and their feet thereat: ^c40v31

[Exodus 40:32](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p32#p32) When they went into the tent of the congregation, and when they came near unto the altar, they washed; as the LORD commanded Moses. ^c40v32

[Exodus 40:33](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p33#p33) And he reared up the court round about the tabernacle and the altar, and set up the hanging of the court gate.  So Moses finished the work. ^c40v33

[Exodus 40:34](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p34#p34) ¶ Then a cloud covered the tent of the congregation, and the glory of the LORD filled the tabernacle. ^c40v34

[Exodus 40:35](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p35#p35) And Moses was not able to enter into the tent of the congregation, because the cloud abode thereon, and the glory of the LORD filled the tabernacle. ^c40v35

[Exodus 40:36](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p36#p36) And when the cloud was taken up from over the tabernacle, the children of Israel went onward in all their journeys: ^c40v36

[Exodus 40:37](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p37#p37) But if the cloud were not taken up, then they journeyed not till the day that it was taken up. ^c40v37

[Exodus 40:38](https://churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scriptures/ot/ex/40?lang=eng&id=p38#p38) For the cloud of the LORD was upon the tabernacle by day, and fire was on it by night, in the sight of all the house of Israel, throughout all their journeys. ^c40v38
